View All Recent Stories At the grassroots level, [ideological liberation used to mean] freedom, tolerance, diversity, and the breaking open of forbidden zones—new subjects were up for discussion, new authorities were open for questioning, new essays could be published." — From a now-deleted WeChat essay by blogger Feng Hongping, ruminating on how the CCP has cheapened the term “ideological liberation,” having reduced it to mean submission to the Party line. Feng was responding to a recently announced campaign by Hunan’s Provincial Party Committee that frames “ideological liberation” as slavish adherence to Xi Jinping Thought.
